		"2"
		{
			"command"	"play buttons/button14; say !remove; show_menu TurretRemove"
			"label"		" Remove One By One"
		}
		"3"
		{
			"command"	"play buttons/button14; say !remove all; show_menu TurretRemove"
			"label"		" Remove All"
		}
		"8"
		{
			"command"	"play buttons/button14; show_menu Turret"
			"label"		" << Back"
		}
		"0"
		{
			"command"	"play buttons/button14"
			"label"		" Exit"
		}
	}
